reasoning (7599 chars)
Still very slow: shape 0 is 2.28ms. The non-unrolled bitonic sort is slow due to loop overhead. I need a different approach. The bitonic sort has too many stages. For top-k, I should use a selection algorithm with O(N log k) complexity, not O(N log^2 N). Let me think about the heap approach again, but implement it efficiently. For k=64, each warp maintains a heap of 64 values. Each new element: compare with heap min, replace if larger. The key is to do this efficiently in parallel. Actually, there's a known efficient GPU top-k algorithm: **radix select**. For each warp/block, count elements with value > threshold, adjust threshold. But implementing radix in CUDA is complex. Alternatively, use **warp-level tournament tree** or **bitonic merge tree**. **Bitonic merge tree for top-k:** 1. Divide row into chunks of size k. 2. Sort each chunk descending (bitonic sort size k). With 32 warps per block, each warp can sort one chunk? Or one block sorts multiple chunks sequentially. 3. Merge sorted chunks in pairs, keeping top k each time. For n=131072, k=64: - Chunks: 2048 chunks of 64. - Each block sorts some chunks. With 1 block per row (batch=1), the block needs to sort 2048 chunks. That's a lot. - Alternatively, use multiple blocks per row. Hmm. For batch=1, we need intra-row parallelism. Use multiple blocks per row, each processing a chunk, then a final reduction. Actually, a better design for large n small batch: - Launch many blocks. Each block handles one chunk of the row (size CHUNK). - Each block sorts its chunk and writes top-k to global memory. - Second kernel: merge all top-k chunks. For n=131072, k=64, CHUNK=4096: - Number of chunks = 32. - Launch 32 blocks. Each sorts 4096 and writes top 64. - Second kernel: merge 32*64=2048 values to top 64. First pass: 32 blocks, each sorting 4096. With 1 block per chunk and 1024 threads, each block sorts its chunk. Sorting 4096 has 78 sub-stages. ~50us per block? Parallel across 32 blocks. ~50us total. Second pass: 1 block sorts 2048 values. ~20us. Total ~70us for shape 0. Much better! For n=8192, k=8, CHUNK=4096? But k=8, chunk should be maybe larger. Actually CHUNK can be fixed at 4096 for all. For n=8192, 2 chunks, 2 blocks. Sort 4096 each, keep top 8. Merge 16 values. Very fast. For n=16384, 4 chunks. For n=12000, 3 chunks (padded to 12288 or handle remainder). For n=4096 k=1, argmax. This two-pass approach is promising. Let me implement it. **Pass 1 kernel:** one block per chunk. - Block sorts CHUNK values descending in shared memory. - Writes top K values and indices to global output arrays at chunk index. - Input: x (B, N). For each row, chunks = ceil(N/CHUNK). - Total blocks = B * chunks. **Pass 2 kernel:** one block per row. - Reads all top-k from chunks (chunks * K values per row). - Sorts them and writes top K. Shared memory for pass 1: CHUNK * 8 bytes. For CHUNK=4096, 32KB. Under 48KB. Shared memory for pass 2: (chunks * K) * 8 bytes. For shape 0, 32*64*8=16KB. For shape 1, 2*8*8=128 bytes. But we need max over all shapes. Max is shape 0: 16KB. Fine. Actually, pass 2 needs to handle variable chunks*K. We can sort up to a max size. For shape 0, chunks=32, K=64, total=2048. Power of 2. Good. But for shape 1 (n=8192, K=8), chunks=2, total=16. We can still allocate shared mem for max and only use part. Or use dynamic. To keep it simple, allocate shared mem based on actual total per row. Implementation details: Pass 1: ```cuda template <int K, int CHUNK> __global__ void topk_pass1(const float* x, float* chunk_val, int* chunk_idx, int B, int N) { int row = blockIdx.y; // or blockIdx.x / chunks int chunk = blockIdx.x % chunks; ... } ``` Or use 1D grid: block_id = row * chunks + chunk. row = block_id / chunks, chunk = block_id % chunks. Pass 2: ```cuda template <int K, int CHUNK> __global__ void topk_pass2(const float* chunk_val, const int* chunk_idx, float* out_val, int64_t* out_idx, int B, int N, int chunks) { int row = blockIdx.x; int total = chunks * K; // load into shared mem // sort total (must be power of 2) // write top K } ``` But total must be power of 2 for bitonic sort. For shape 0, 32*64=2048 (power of 2). For shape 1, 2*8=16 (power of 2). For shape 2, 4*32=128 (power of 2). For shape 3, 3*16=48 (not power of 2). For shape 4, k=1 handled separately. For shape 3 (n=12000, k=16), CHUNK=4096, chunks=3 (since 12000/4096 = 2.9, ceil=3). Total=48. Not power of 2. We can pad to 64. So in pass 2, allocate shared mem for next power of 2 >= chunks*K, pad with -inf. But the template needs the power-of-2 size. We can compute it at runtime or use a template parameter. Alternatively, in pass 2, we can use a different approach for non-power-of-2: sort in shared memory with size = next_pow2(chunks*K). We can pass this as a template parameter by switch cases. Actually, simpler: in pass 2, use the same `bitonic_sort_desc` template but with N = next power of 2. For shape 3, N=64. We can have a dispatch switch for pass 2 based on total size. +// Partial bitonic sort: after completion, the first K entries contain the K
+// largest values in descending order.  Comparisons entirely within the tail
+// (both indices >= K) are skipped.
+template <int N, int K>
+__device__ __forceinline__ void bitonic_partial_sort_desc(float* __restrict__ val,
+                                                          int*   __restrict__ idx) {
+    for (int k = 2; k <= N; k <<= 1) {
+        for (int j = k >> 1; j > 0; j >>= 1) {
+            int tid = threadIdx.x;
+            for (int i = tid; i < N; i += blockDim.x) {
+                int lo = i;
+                int hi = i ^ j;
+                if (hi > lo && (lo < K || hi < K)) {
+                    if ((lo & k) == 0) {
+                        if (val[lo] < val[hi]) {
+                            float tv = val[lo]; val[lo] = val[hi]; val[hi] = tv;
+                            int ti = idx[lo]; idx[lo] = idx[hi]; idx[hi] = ti;
+                        }
+                    } else {
+                        if (val[lo] > val[hi]) {
+                            float tv = val[lo]; val[lo] = val[hi]; val[hi] = tv;
+                            int ti = idx[lo]; idx[lo] = idx[hi]; idx[hi] = ti;
+                        }
+                    }
+                }
+            }
+            __syncthreads();
+        }
+    }
+}

Insert each element: if > heap min, replace min and sift down. But with multiple threads, we need synchronization. Options: 1. Single thread processes all elements (serial). Simple but slow. 2. For top-k, we want the K largest. Use min-heap of size K: root is the K-th largest. Any new value > root replaces root and sifts down. After all elements, heap contains top K (unsorted). Sort heap before writing. Sift down for min-heap: ```cuda void sift_down(int pos, float* heap_val, int* heap_idx, int K) { while (true) { int left = 2*pos + 1; int right = 2*pos + 2; int smallest = pos; if (left < K && heap_val[left] < heap_val[smallest]) smallest = left; if (right < K && heap_val[right] < heap_val[smallest]) smallest = right; if (smallest == pos) break; swap(heap_val[pos], heap_val[smallest]); swap(heap_idx[pos], heap_idx[smallest]); pos = smallest; } } ``` Build heap initially with first K elements: for i = K/2 - 1 down to 0, sift_down(i). Then for each remaining element, if > heap[0], replace and sift_down(0). After processing, sort heap descending (since min-heap, sort descending gives top-k sorted). For K=64, sorting heap is cheap (bitonic sort 64 or just insertion sort). Let me implement a `block_heap_topk` kernel. Actually, I can use this for pass 1. Pass 2 still uses sort of candidates. +__device__ __forceinline__ void heap_swap(float& v1, int& i1, float& v2, int& i2) {
+    float tv = v1; v1 = v2; v2 = tv;
+    int ti = i1; i1 = i2; i2 = ti;
+}
+
+template <int K>
+__device__ __forceinline__ void heap_sift_down(int pos, float* heap_val, int* heap_idx) {
+    while (true) {
+        int left = 2 * pos + 1;
+        int right = 2 * pos + 2;
+        int smallest = pos;
+        if (left < K && heap_val[left] < heap_val[smallest]) smallest = left;
+        if (right < K && heap_val[right] < heap_val[smallest]) smallest = right;
+        if (smallest == pos) break;
+        heap_swap(heap_val[pos], heap_idx[pos], heap_val[smallest], heap_idx[smallest]);
+        pos = smallest;
+    }
+}
+
+template <int K>
+__device__ __forceinline__ void heap_sort_desc(float* heap_val, int* heap_idx) {
+    // Selection-sort style in-place descending sort of the K heap entries.
+    for (int i = 0; i < K - 1; ++i) {
+        int best = i;
+        for (int j = i + 1; j < K; ++j) {
+            if (heap_val[j] > heap_val[best]) best = j;
+        }
+        if (best != i) heap_swap(heap_val[i], heap_idx[i], heap_val[best], heap_idx[best]);
+    }
+}

import torch
from torch.utils.cpp_extension import load_inline

src = r'''
#include <cuda_runtime.h>
#include <torch/extension.h>

template <int N>
__device__ void bitonic_sort_desc(float* val, int* idx) {
    for (int k = 2; k <= N; k <<= 1) {
        for (int j = k >> 1; j > 0; j >>= 1) {
            int tid = threadIdx.x;
            for (int i = tid; i < N; i += blockDim.x) {
                int lo = i;
                int hi = i ^ j;
                if (hi > lo) {
                    if ((lo & k) == 0) {
                        if (val[lo] < val[hi]) {
                            float tv = val[lo]; val[lo] = val[hi]; val[hi] = tv;
                            int ti = idx[lo]; idx[lo] = idx[hi]; idx[hi] = ti;
                        }
                    } else {
                        if (val[lo] > val[hi]) {
                            float tv = val[lo]; val[lo] = val[hi]; val[hi] = tv;
                            int ti = idx[lo]; idx[lo] = idx[hi]; idx[hi] = ti;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            __syncthreads();
        }
    }
}

__global__ void test(const float* in, float* out) {
    extern __shared__ char smem[];
    float* s = (float*)smem;
    int* idx = (int*)(s + 4096);
    for (int i = threadIdx.x; i < 4096; i += blockDim.x) {
        s[i] = in[i];
        idx[i] = i;
    }
    __syncthreads();
    bitonic_sort_desc<4096>(s, idx);
    for (int i = threadIdx.x; i < 4096; i += blockDim.x) {
        out[i] = s[i];
    }
}

torch::Tensor run_test(torch::Tensor x) {
    auto out = torch::empty_like(x);
    test<<<1, 1024, 4096*(sizeof(float)+sizeof(int))>>>(x.data_ptr<float>(), out.data_ptr<float>());
    return out;
}
'''
cpp = r'''
#include <torch/extension.h>
torch::Tensor run_test(torch::Tensor x);
'''
mod = load_inline(name='test_block4096', cpp_sources=cpp, cuda_sources=src,
                  functions=['run_test'], extra_cuda_cflags=['-O3'], verbose=False)

x = torch.randn(4096).cuda()
out = mod.run_test(x)
ref, _ = torch.sort(x, descending=True)
print('match 4096 block1024:', torch.allclose(out, ref, atol=1e-5, rtol=1e-5))
print('max diff:', (out - ref).abs().max().item())

import torch
from torch.utils.cpp_extension import load_inline

src = r'''
#include <cuda_runtime.h>
#include <torch/extension.h>

template <int N>
__device__ void bitonic_sort_desc(float* val, int* idx) {
    for (int k = 2; k <= N; k <<= 1) {
        for (int j = k >> 1; j > 0; j >>= 1) {
            int tid = threadIdx.x;
            for (int i = tid; i < N; i += blockDim.x) {
                int lo = i;
                int hi = i ^ j;
                if (hi > lo) {
                    if ((lo & k) == 0) {
                        if (val[lo] < val[hi]) {
                            float tv = val[lo]; val[lo] = val[hi]; val[hi] = tv;
                            int ti = idx[lo]; idx[lo] = idx[hi]; idx[hi] = ti;
                        }
                    } else {
                        if (val[lo] > val[hi]) {
                            float tv = val[lo]; val[lo] = val[hi]; val[hi] = tv;
                            int ti = idx[lo]; idx[lo] = idx[hi]; idx[hi] = ti;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
            __syncthreads();
        }
    }
}

__global__ void test(const float* in, float* out) {
    extern __shared__ char smem[];
    float* s = (float*)smem;
    int* idx = (int*)(s + 128);
    for (int i = threadIdx.x; i < 128; i += blockDim.x) {
        s[i] = in[i];
        idx[i] = i;
    }
    __syncthreads();
    bitonic_sort_desc<128>(s, idx);
    for (int i = threadIdx.x; i < 128; i += blockDim.x) {
        out[i] = s[i];
    }
}

torch::Tensor run_test(torch::Tensor x) {
    auto out = torch::empty_like(x);
    test<<<1, 1024, 128*(sizeof(float)+sizeof(int))>>>(x.data_ptr<float>(), out.data_ptr<float>());
    return out;
}
'''
cpp = r'''
#include <torch/extension.h>
torch::Tensor run_test(torch::Tensor x);
'''
mod = load_inline(name='test_block128', cpp_sources=cpp, cuda_sources=src,
                  functions=['run_test'], extra_cuda_cflags=['-O3'], verbose=False)

x = torch.randn(128).cuda()
out = mod.run_test(x)
ref, _ = torch.sort(x, descending=True)
print('match 128 block1024:', torch.allclose(out, ref, atol=1e-5, rtol=1e-5))
print('max diff:', (out - ref).abs().max().item())

+__device__ __forceinline__ void warp_reduce_argmax(float& v, int& idx) {
+    #pragma unroll
+    for (int offset = 16; offset > 0; offset >>= 1) {
+        float other_v = __shfl_down_sync(0xFFFFFFFF, v, offset);
+        int other_i = __shfl_down_sync(0xFFFFFFFF, idx, offset);
+        if (other_v > v) {
+            v = other_v;
+            idx = other_i;
+        }
+    }
+}

import torch
x = torch.randn(2048)
base = 0
s_val = x.clone()
s_idx = torch.arange(2048)
K = 64
for pos in range(K):
    best_v, best_i = -float('inf'), 0
    for i in range(pos, 2048):
        if s_val[i] > best_v:
            best_v = s_val[i]
            best_i = i
    target_v, target_i = s_val[pos].item(), s_idx[pos].item()
    s_val[pos] = best_v
    s_idx[pos] = best_i
    s_val[best_i] = target_v
    s_idx[best_i] = target_i

ref, _ = torch.sort(x, descending=True)
print('match:', torch.allclose(s_val[:K], ref[:K], atol=1e-5))
print('maxdiff:', (s_val[:K] - ref[:K]).abs().max().item())
" 2>&1 | tail -5

import torch
from torch.utils.cpp_extension import load_inline

src = r'''
#include <cuda_runtime.h>
#include <cub/block/block_radix_sort.cuh>
#include <torch/extension.h>

#define BLOCK_THREADS 1024
#define ITEMS_PER_THREAD 4

typedef cub::BlockRadixSort<float, BLOCK_THREADS, ITEMS_PER_THREAD, int> BlockSort;

__global__ void test(const float* in, float* out) {
    __shared__ typename BlockSort::TempStorage temp_storage;
    float thread_keys[ITEMS_PER_THREAD];
    int thread_values[ITEMS_PER_THREAD];
    int tid = threadIdx.x;
    #pragma unroll
    for (int i = 0; i < ITEMS_PER_THREAD; ++i) {
        int idx = tid + i * BLOCK_THREADS;
        thread_keys[i] = in[idx];
        thread_values[i] = idx;
    }
    BlockSort(temp_storage).SortDescendingBlockedToStriped(thread_keys, thread_values);
    #pragma unroll
    for (int i = 0; i < ITEMS_PER_THREAD; ++i) {
        int idx = tid + i * BLOCK_THREADS;
        out[idx] = thread_keys[i];
    }
}

torch::Tensor run_test(torch::Tensor x) {
    auto out = torch::empty_like(x);
    test<<<1, BLOCK_THREADS>>>(x.data_ptr<float>(), out.data_ptr<float>());
    return out;
}
'''
cpp = r'''
#include <torch/extension.h>
torch::Tensor run_test(torch::Tensor x);
'''
mod = load_inline(name='test_cub', cpp_sources=cpp, cuda_sources=src,
                  functions=['run_test'], extra_cuda_cflags=['-O3'], verbose=False)

x = torch.randn(4096).cuda()
out = mod.run_test(x)
ref, _ = torch.sort(x, descending=True)
print('match 4096 CUB:', torch.allclose(out, ref, atol=1e-5, rtol=1e-5))
print('max diff:', (out - ref).abs().max().item())

import torch
from torch.utils.cpp_extension import load_inline

src = r'''
#include <cuda_runtime.h>
#include <cub/block/block_radix_sort.cuh>
#include <torch/extension.h>

#define BLOCK_THREADS 1024
#define ITEMS_PER_THREAD 8

typedef cub::BlockRadixSort<float, BLOCK_THREADS, ITEMS_PER_THREAD, int> BlockSort;

__global__ void test(const float* in, float* out) {
    __shared__ typename BlockSort::TempStorage temp_storage;
    float thread_keys[ITEMS_PER_THREAD];
    int thread_values[ITEMS_PER_THREAD];
    int tid = threadIdx.x;
    #pragma unroll
    for (int i = 0; i < ITEMS_PER_THREAD; ++i) {
        int idx = tid + i * BLOCK_THREADS;
        thread_keys[i] = in[idx];
        thread_values[i] = idx;
    }
    BlockSort(temp_storage).SortDescendingBlockedToStriped(thread_keys, thread_values);
    #pragma unroll
    for (int i = 0; i < ITEMS_PER_THREAD; ++i) {
        int idx = tid + i * BLOCK_THREADS;
        out[idx] = thread_keys[i];
    }
}

torch::Tensor run_test(torch::Tensor x) {
    auto out = torch::empty_like(x);
    test<<<1, BLOCK_THREADS>>>(x.data_ptr<float>(), out.data_ptr<float>());
    return out;
}
'''
cpp = r'''
#include <torch/extension.h>
torch::Tensor run_test(torch::Tensor x);
'''
try:
    mod = load_inline(name='test_cub8192', cpp_sources=cpp, cuda_sources=src,
                      functions=['run_test'], extra_cuda_cflags=['-O3'], verbose=False)
    x = torch.randn(8192).cuda()
    out = mod.run_test(x)
    ref, _ = torch.sort(x, descending=True)
    print('match 8192 CUB:', torch.allclose(out, ref, atol=1e-5, rtol=1e-5))
    print('max diff:', (out - ref).abs().max().item())
except Exception as e:
    print('FAIL:', e)

cat > /tmp/test_cub512.py << 'PYEOF'
import torch
from torch.utils.cpp_extension import load_inline

src = r'''
#include <cuda_runtime.h>
#include <cub/block/block_radix_sort.cuh>
#include <torch/extension.h>

#define BLOCK_THREADS 512
#define ITEMS_PER_THREAD 16

typedef cub::BlockRadixSort<float, BLOCK_THREADS, ITEMS_PER_THREAD, int> BlockSort;

__global__ void test(const float* in, float* out) {
    __shared__ typename BlockSort::TempStorage temp_storage;
    float thread_keys[ITEMS_PER_THREAD];
    int thread_values[ITEMS_PER_THREAD];
    int tid = threadIdx.x;
    #pragma unroll
    for (int i = 0; i < ITEMS_PER_THREAD; ++i) {
        int idx = tid + i * BLOCK_THREADS;
        thread_keys[i] = in[idx];
        thread_values[i] = idx;
    }
    BlockSort(temp_storage).SortDescendingBlockedToStriped(thread_keys, thread_values);
    #pragma unroll
    for (int i = 0; i < ITEMS_PER_THREAD; ++i) {
        int idx = tid + i * BLOCK_THREADS;
        out[idx] = thread_keys[i];
    }
}

torch::Tensor run_test(torch::Tensor x) {
    auto out = torch::empty_like(x);
    test<<<1, BLOCK_THREADS>>>(x.data_ptr<float>(), out.data_ptr<float>());
    return out;
}
'''
cpp = r'''
#include <torch/extension.h>
torch::Tensor run_test(torch::Tensor x);
'''
try:
    mod = load_inline(name='test_cub512', cpp_sources=cpp, cuda_sources=src,
                      functions=['run_test'], extra_cuda_cflags=['-O3'], verbose=False)
    x = torch.randn(8192).cuda()
    out = mod.run_test(x)
    ref, _ = torch.sort(x, descending=True)
    print('match 8192 CUB512x16:', torch.allclose(out, ref, atol=1e-5, rtol=1e-5))
    print('max diff:', (out - ref).abs().max().item())
except Exception as e:
    print('FAIL:', e)

import torch
import solution
from shapes import SHAPES

device = torch.device('cuda:0')
for shape in SHAPES:
    b,n,k = shape['batch'], shape['n'], shape['k']
    m = solution.Model(b,n,k).cuda().eval()
    x = torch.randn(b,n,device=device)
    cm = torch.compile(m, mode='reduce-overhead')
    for _ in range(15): cm(x)
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    s = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
    e = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
    s.record()
    for _ in range(50): cm(x)
    e.record()
    torch.cuda.synchronize()
    ms = s.elapsed_time(e) / 50
    bytes_moved = b*n*4 + b*k*(4+8)
    gbps = bytes_moved / (ms * 1e6)
